(** **********************************************************

Contents:

- Definition of slice precategories, C/x (assumes that C has homsets)

- Isos in slice categories

- Monics in slice categories

- Epis in slice categories

- Proof that the forgetful functor [slicecat_to_cat] : C/x → C is
  a left adjoint if C has binary products ([is_left_adjoint_slicecat_to_cat])

- Proof that C/x is a univalent_category if C is

- Proof that any morphism C[x,y] induces a functor from C/x to C/y
  ([slicecat_functor])

- Colimits in slice categories ([slice_precat_colims])

- Binary products in slice categories of categories with pullbacks
  ([BinProducts_slice_precat])

- Binary coproducts in slice categories of categories with binary
  coproducts ([BinCoproducts_slice_precat])

- Coproducts in slice categories of categories with coproducts
  ([Coproducts_slice_precat])

- Initial object in slice categories with initial object
  ([Initial_slice_precat])

- Terminal object in slice categories ([Terminal_slice_precat])

- Base change functor ([base_change_functor]) and proof that
  it is right adjoint to slicecat_functor

- Pullbacks ([pullback_to_slice_pullback])

************************************************************)

Local Open Scope cat.

(** * Definition of slice categories *)
(** Given a category C and x : obj C. The slice category C/x is given by:

- obj C/x: pairs (a,f) where f : a -> x

- morphism (a,f) -> (b,g): morphism h : a -> b with
<<
           h
       a - - -> b
       |       /
       |     /
     f |   / g
       | /
       v
       x
>>
    where h · g = f

*)
Section slice_precat_def.

Context (C : category) (x : C).

(* Accessor functions *)
Definition slicecat_ob := ∑ a, C⟦a,x⟧.
Definition slicecat_mor (f g : slicecat_ob) := ∑ h, pr2 f = h · pr2 g.

Definition slicecat_ob_object (f : slicecat_ob) : ob C := pr1 f.

Definition slicecat_ob_morphism (f : slicecat_ob) : C⟦slicecat_ob_object f, x⟧ := pr2 f.

(* Accessor functions *)
Definition slicecat_mor_morphism {f g : slicecat_ob} (h : slicecat_mor f g) :
  C⟦slicecat_ob_object f, slicecat_ob_object g⟧ := pr1 h.

Definition slicecat_mor_comm {f g : slicecat_ob} (h : slicecat_mor f g) :
  (slicecat_ob_morphism f) = (slicecat_mor_morphism h) · (slicecat_ob_morphism g) := pr2 h.

Definition slice_precat_ob_mor : precategory_ob_mor := (slicecat_ob,,slicecat_mor).

Definition id_slice_precat (c : slice_precat_ob_mor) : c --> c :=
  tpair _ _ (!(id_left (pr2 c))).


C: category
x: C
a, b, c: slice_precat_ob_mor
f: slice_precat_ob_mor ⟦ a, b ⟧
g: slice_precat_ob_mor ⟦ b, c ⟧
pr2 a = pr1 f · pr1 g · pr2 c


C: category
x: C
a, b, c: slice_precat_ob_mor
f: slice_precat_ob_mor ⟦ a, b ⟧
g: slice_precat_ob_mor ⟦ b, c ⟧
pr2 a = pr1 f · pr1 g · pr2 c

  
C: category
x: C
a, b, c: slice_precat_ob_mor
f: slice_precat_ob_mor ⟦ a, b ⟧
g: slice_precat_ob_mor ⟦ b, c ⟧
pr2 a = pr1 f · pr2 b

  exact (pr2 f).
Qed.

Definition comp_slice_precat (a b c : slice_precat_ob_mor)
                             (f : a --> b) (g : b --> c) : a --> c :=
  (pr1 f · pr1 g,,comp_slice_precat_subproof _ _).

Definition slice_precat_data : precategory_data :=
  make_precategory_data _ id_slice_precat comp_slice_precat.


C: category
x: C
is_precategory slice_precat_data


C: category
x: C
is_precategory slice_precat_data


C: category
x: C
∏ (a b : slicecat_ob) (f : slicecat_mor a b),
identity a · f = f
C: category
x: C
∏ (a b : slicecat_ob) (f : slicecat_mor a b),
f · identity b = f
C: category
x: C
∏ (a b c d : slicecat_ob) (f : slicecat_mor a b)
(g : slicecat_mor b c) (h : slicecat_mor c d),
f · (g · h) = f · g · h
C: category
x: C
∏ (a b c d : slicecat_ob) (f : slicecat_mor a b)
(g : slicecat_mor b c) (h : slicecat_mor c d),
f · g · h = f · (g · h)


C: category
x: C
∏ (a b : slicecat_ob) (f : slicecat_mor a b),
identity a · f = f
 
C: category
x: C
a, b: slicecat_ob
f: slicecat_mor a b
identity a · f = f

  
C: category
x: C
a, b: slicecat_ob
h: C ⟦ pr1 a, pr1 b ⟧
hP: pr2 a = h · pr2 b
identity a · (h,, hP) = h,, hP

  apply subtypePairEquality; [ intro; apply C | apply id_left ].

C: category
x: C
∏ (a b : slicecat_ob) (f : slicecat_mor a b),
f · identity b = f
 
C: category
x: C
a, b: slicecat_ob
f: slicecat_mor a b
f · identity b = f

  
C: category
x: C
a, b: slicecat_ob
h: C ⟦ pr1 a, pr1 b ⟧
hP: pr2 a = h · pr2 b
(h,, hP) · identity b = h,, hP

  apply subtypePairEquality; [ intro; apply C | apply id_right ].

C: category
x: C
∏ (a b c d : slicecat_ob) (f : slicecat_mor a b)
(g : slicecat_mor b c) (h : slicecat_mor c d),
f · (g · h) = f · g · h
 
C: category
x: C
a, b, c, d: slicecat_ob
f: slicecat_mor a b
g: slicecat_mor b c
h: slicecat_mor c d
f · (g · h) = f · g · h

  apply subtypePairEquality; [ intro; apply C | apply assoc ].

C: category
x: C
∏ (a b c d : slicecat_ob) (f : slicecat_mor a b)
(g : slicecat_mor b c) (h : slicecat_mor c d),
f · g · h = f · (g · h)
 
C: category
x: C
a, b, c, d: slicecat_ob
f: slicecat_mor a b
g: slicecat_mor b c
h: slicecat_mor c d
f · g · h = f · (g · h)

  apply subtypePairEquality; [ intro; apply C | apply assoc' ].
Qed.

Definition slice_precat : precategory :=
  (_,,is_precategory_slice_precat_data).


C: category
x: C
has_homsets slice_precat


C: category
x: C
has_homsets slice_precat


C: category
x: C
a, b: slice_precat
isaset (slice_precat ⟦ a, b ⟧)


C: category
x, a: C
f: C ⟦ a, x ⟧
b: C
g: C ⟦ b, x ⟧
isaset (slicecat_mor (a,, f) (b,, g))


C: category
x, a: C
f: C ⟦ a, x ⟧
b: C
g: C ⟦ b, x ⟧
h: C ⟦ pr1 (a,, f), pr1 (b,, g) ⟧
isofhlevel 2 (pr2 (a,, f) = h · pr2 (b,, g))

apply isasetaprop; apply C.
Qed.

  Definition slice_cat : category := make_category _ has_homsets_slice_precat.


End slice_precat_def.

Section slice_precat_theory.

  Context (C : category)
          (x : C).


Local Notation "C / X" := (slice_cat C X).


C: category
x: C
af, bg: C / x
f, g: C / x ⟦ af, bg ⟧
pr1 f = pr1 g → f = g


C: category
x: C
af, bg: C / x
f, g: C / x ⟦ af, bg ⟧
pr1 f = pr1 g → f = g

intro heq; apply (total2_paths_f heq); apply C.
Qed.


C: category
x: C
af, bg: C / x
f, g: C / x ⟦ af, bg ⟧
isweq (eq_mor_slicecat af bg f g)


C: category
x: C
af, bg: C / x
f, g: C / x ⟦ af, bg ⟧
isweq (eq_mor_slicecat af bg f g)

  
C: category
x: C
af, bg: C / x
f, g: C / x ⟦ af, bg ⟧
f = g → pr1 f = pr1 g
C: category
x: C
af, bg: C / x
f, g: C / x ⟦ af, bg ⟧
isaprop (pr1 f = pr1 g)
C: category
x: C
af, bg: C / x
f, g: C / x ⟦ af, bg ⟧
isaprop (f = g)

  
C: category
x: C
af, bg: C / x
f, g: C / x ⟦ af, bg ⟧
f = g → pr1 f = pr1 g
 apply maponpaths.
  
C: category
x: C
af, bg: C / x
f, g: C / x ⟦ af, bg ⟧
isaprop (pr1 f = pr1 g)
 apply C.
  
C: category
x: C
af, bg: C / x
f, g: C / x ⟦ af, bg ⟧
isaprop (f = g)
 apply has_homsets_slice_precat.
Qed.

Definition  eq_mor_slicecat_weq (af bg : C / x) (f g : C/x⟦af,bg⟧) :
  (pr1 f = pr1 g ≃ f = g) := make_weq _ (eq_mor_slicecat_isweq af bg f g).


(** ** Isos in slice categories *)


C: category
x: C
af, bg: C / x
f, g: z_iso af bg
pr1 f = pr1 g → f = g


C: category
x: C
af, bg: C / x
f, g: z_iso af bg
pr1 f = pr1 g → f = g


C: category
x: C
af, bg: C / x
f: C / x ⟦ af, bg ⟧
fP: is_z_isomorphism f
g: C / x ⟦ af, bg ⟧
gP: is_z_isomorphism g
eq: pr1 (f,, fP) = pr1 (g,, gP)
f,, fP = g,, gP


C: category
x: C
af, bg: C / x
f: C / x ⟦ af, bg ⟧
fP: is_z_isomorphism f
g: C / x ⟦ af, bg ⟧
gP: is_z_isomorphism g
eq: pr1 (f,, fP) = pr1 (g,, gP)
isPredicate
  (λ f : C / x ⟦ af, bg ⟧, is_z_isomorphism f)

intro; apply isaprop_is_z_isomorphism.
Qed.

(** It suffices that the underlying morphism is an iso to get an iso in
    the slice category *)

C: category
x: C
af, bg: C / x
h: C / x ⟦ af, bg ⟧
isoh: is_z_isomorphism (pr1 h)
is_z_isomorphism h


C: category
x: C
af, bg: C / x
h: C / x ⟦ af, bg ⟧
isoh: is_z_isomorphism (pr1 h)
is_z_isomorphism h


C: category
x: C
af, bg: C / x
h: C / x ⟦ af, bg ⟧
hinv: C ⟦ pr1 bg, pr1 af ⟧
h1: pr1 h · hinv = identity (pr1 af)
h2: hinv · pr1 h = identity (pr1 bg)
is_z_isomorphism h


C: category
x: C
af, bg: C / x
h: C / x ⟦ af, bg ⟧
hinv: C ⟦ pr1 bg, pr1 af ⟧
h1: pr1 h · hinv = identity (pr1 af)
h2: hinv · pr1 h = identity (pr1 bg)
hinv · pr2 af = pr2 bg
C: category
x: C
af, bg: C / x
h: C / x ⟦ af, bg ⟧
hinv: C ⟦ pr1 bg, pr1 af ⟧
h1: pr1 h · hinv = identity (pr1 af)
h2: hinv · pr1 h = identity (pr1 bg)
pinv: hinv · pr2 af = pr2 bg
is_z_isomorphism h


C: category
x: C
af, bg: C / x
h: C / x ⟦ af, bg ⟧
hinv: C ⟦ pr1 bg, pr1 af ⟧
h1: pr1 h · hinv = identity (pr1 af)
h2: hinv · pr1 h = identity (pr1 bg)
hinv · pr2 af = pr2 bg
 rewrite <- id_left, <- h2, <- assoc, (!(pr2 h)); apply idpath. 
C: category
x: C
af, bg: C / x
h: C / x ⟦ af, bg ⟧
hinv: C ⟦ pr1 bg, pr1 af ⟧
h1: pr1 h · hinv = identity (pr1 af)
h2: hinv · pr1 h = identity (pr1 bg)
pinv: hinv · pr2 af = pr2 bg
is_z_isomorphism h


C: category
x: C
af, bg: C / x
h: C / x ⟦ af, bg ⟧
hinv: C ⟦ pr1 bg, pr1 af ⟧
h1: pr1 h · hinv = identity (pr1 af)
h2: hinv · pr1 h = identity (pr1 bg)
pinv: hinv · pr2 af = pr2 bg
is_inverse_in_precat h (hinv,, ! pinv)

split; (apply subtypePairEquality; [ intro; apply C |]); assumption.
Defined.

(** An iso in the slice category gives an iso in the base category *)

C: category
x: C
af, bg: C / x
h: C / x ⟦ af, bg ⟧
p: is_z_isomorphism h
is_z_isomorphism (pr1 h)


C: category
x: C
af, bg: C / x
h: C / x ⟦ af, bg ⟧
p: is_z_isomorphism h
is_z_isomorphism (pr1 h)


C: category
x: C
af, bg: C / x
h: C / x ⟦ af, bg ⟧
hinv: C / x ⟦ bg, af ⟧
h1: h · hinv = identity af
h2: hinv · h = identity bg
is_z_isomorphism (pr1 h)


C: category
x: C
af, bg: C / x
h: C / x ⟦ af, bg ⟧
hinv: C / x ⟦ bg, af ⟧
h1: h · hinv = identity af
h2: hinv · h = identity bg
pr1 h · pr1 hinv = identity (pr1 af)
C: category
x: C
af, bg: C / x
h: C / x ⟦ af, bg ⟧
hinv: C / x ⟦ bg, af ⟧
h1: h · hinv = identity af
h2: hinv · h = identity bg
pr1 hinv · pr1 h = identity (pr1 bg)


C: category
x: C
af, bg: C / x
h: C / x ⟦ af, bg ⟧
hinv: C / x ⟦ bg, af ⟧
h1: h · hinv = identity af
h2: hinv · h = identity bg
pr1 h · pr1 hinv = identity (pr1 af)
 apply (maponpaths pr1 h1).

C: category
x: C
af, bg: C / x
h: C / x ⟦ af, bg ⟧
hinv: C / x ⟦ bg, af ⟧
h1: h · hinv = identity af
h2: hinv · h = identity bg
pr1 hinv · pr1 h = identity (pr1 bg)
 apply (maponpaths pr1 h2).
Defined.


C: category
x: C
af, bg: C / x
z_iso af bg
≃ (∑ h : z_iso (pr1 af) (pr1 bg), pr2 af = h · pr2 bg)


C: category
x: C
af, bg: C / x
z_iso af bg
≃ (∑ h : z_iso (pr1 af) (pr1 bg), pr2 af = h · pr2 bg)

  
C: category
x: C
af, bg: C / x
(∑ (x0 : C ⟦ pr1 af, pr1 bg ⟧)
 (p : pr2 af = x0 · pr2 bg), is_z_isomorphism (x0,, p))
≃ (∑ h : z_iso (pr1 af) (pr1 bg), pr2 af = h · pr2 bg)

  
C: category
x: C
af, bg: C / x
(∑ h : z_iso (pr1 af) (pr1 bg), pr2 af = h · pr2 bg)
≃ (∑ (x0 : C ⟦ pr1 af, pr1 bg ⟧)
   (p : pr2 af = x0 · pr2 bg),
   is_z_isomorphism (x0,, p))

  
C: category
x: C
af, bg: C / x
(∑ (x0 : C ⟦ pr1 af, pr1 bg ⟧)
 (p : is_z_isomorphism x0), pr2 af = (x0,, p) · pr2 bg)
≃ (∑ (x0 : C ⟦ pr1 af, pr1 bg ⟧)
   (p : pr2 af = x0 · pr2 bg),
   is_z_isomorphism (x0,, p))

  
C: category
x: C
af, bg: C / x
h: C ⟦ pr1 af, pr1 bg ⟧
(∑ _ : is_z_isomorphism h, pr2 af = h · pr2 bg)
≃ (∑ p : pr2 af = h · pr2 bg, is_z_isomorphism (h,, p))

  
C: category
x: C
af, bg: C / x
h: C ⟦ pr1 af, pr1 bg ⟧
pr2 af = h · pr2 bg × is_z_isomorphism h
≃ (∑ p : pr2 af = h · pr2 bg, is_z_isomorphism (h,, p))

  
C: category
x: C
af, bg: C / x
h: C ⟦ pr1 af, pr1 bg ⟧
p: pr2 af = h · pr2 bg
is_z_isomorphism h ≃ is_z_isomorphism (h,, p)

  
C: category
x: C
af, bg: C / x
h: C ⟦ pr1 af, pr1 bg ⟧
p: pr2 af = h · pr2 bg
is_z_isomorphism h → is_z_isomorphism (h,, p)
C: category
x: C
af, bg: C / x
h: C ⟦ pr1 af, pr1 bg ⟧
p: pr2 af = h · pr2 bg
is_z_isomorphism (h,, p) → is_z_isomorphism h
C: category
x: C
af, bg: C / x
h: C ⟦ pr1 af, pr1 bg ⟧
p: pr2 af = h · pr2 bg
isaprop (is_z_isomorphism h)
C: category
x: C
af, bg: C / x
h: C ⟦ pr1 af, pr1 bg ⟧
p: pr2 af = h · pr2 bg
isaprop (is_z_isomorphism (h,, p))

  
C: category
x: C
af, bg: C / x
h: C ⟦ pr1 af, pr1 bg ⟧
p: pr2 af = h · pr2 bg
is_z_isomorphism h → is_z_isomorphism (h,, p)
 intro hp; apply z_iso_to_slice_precat_z_iso; assumption.
  
C: category
x: C
af, bg: C / x
h: C ⟦ pr1 af, pr1 bg ⟧
p: pr2 af = h · pr2 bg
is_z_isomorphism (h,, p) → is_z_isomorphism h
 intro hp; apply (slice_precat_z_iso_to_z_iso _ _ _ hp).
  
C: category
x: C
af, bg: C / x
h: C ⟦ pr1 af, pr1 bg ⟧
p: pr2 af = h · pr2 bg
isaprop (is_z_isomorphism h)
 apply isaprop_is_z_isomorphism.
  
C: category
x: C
af, bg: C / x
h: C ⟦ pr1 af, pr1 bg ⟧
p: pr2 af = h · pr2 bg
isaprop (is_z_isomorphism (h,, p))
 apply (isaprop_is_z_isomorphism(C:= C / x)).
Defined.

(** ** Monics in slice categories *)

(** It suffices that the underlying morphism is an monic to get an monic in
    the slice category *)

C: category
x: C
a, b: C / x
h: C / x ⟦ a, b ⟧
monich: isMonic (pr1 h)
isMonic h


C: category
x: C
a, b: C / x
h: C / x ⟦ a, b ⟧
monich: isMonic (pr1 h)
isMonic h

  
C: category
x: C
a, b: C / x
h: C / x ⟦ a, b ⟧
monich: isMonic (pr1 h)
y: C / x
f, g: C / x ⟦ y, a ⟧
eq: f · h = g · h
f = g

  
C: category
x: C
a, b: C / x
h: C / x ⟦ a, b ⟧
monich: isMonic (pr1 h)
y: C / x
f, g: C / x ⟦ y, a ⟧
eq: f · h = g · h
pr1 f · pr1 h = pr1 g · pr1 h

  
C: category
x: C
a, b: C / x
h: C / x ⟦ a, b ⟧
monich: isMonic (pr1 h)
y: C / x
f, g: C / x ⟦ y, a ⟧
eq: f · h = g · h
pr1 (f · h) = pr1 (g · h)

  
C: category
x: C
a, b: C / x
h: C / x ⟦ a, b ⟧
monich: isMonic (pr1 h)
y: C / x
f, g: C / x ⟦ y, a ⟧
eq: f · h = g · h
f · h = g · h

  assumption.
Qed.

(** ** Epis in slice categories *)

(** It suffices that the underlying morphism is an epic to get an epic in
    the slice category *)

C: category
x: C
a, b: C / x
h: C / x ⟦ a, b ⟧
epich: isEpi (pr1 h)
isEpi h


C: category
x: C
a, b: C / x
h: C / x ⟦ a, b ⟧
epich: isEpi (pr1 h)
isEpi h

  
C: category
x: C
a, b: C / x
h: C / x ⟦ a, b ⟧
epich: ∏ (z : C) (g h0 : C ⟦ pr1 b, z ⟧),
pr1 h · g = pr1 h · h0 → g = h0
∏ (z : C / x) (g h0 : C / x ⟦ b, z ⟧),
h · g = h · h0 → g = h0

  
C: category
x: C
a, b: C / x
h: C / x ⟦ a, b ⟧
epich: ∏ (z : C) (g h0 : C ⟦ pr1 b, z ⟧),
pr1 h · g = pr1 h · h0 → g = h0
y: C / x
f, g: C / x ⟦ b, y ⟧
eq: h · f = h · g
f = g

  
C: category
x: C
a, b: C / x
h: C / x ⟦ a, b ⟧
epich: ∏ (z : C) (g h0 : C ⟦ pr1 b, z ⟧),
pr1 h · g = pr1 h · h0 → g = h0
y: C / x
f, g: C / x ⟦ b, y ⟧
eq: h · f = h · g
pr1 h · pr1 f = pr1 h · pr1 g

  
C: category
x: C
a, b: C / x
h: C / x ⟦ a, b ⟧
epich: ∏ (z : C) (g h0 : C ⟦ pr1 b, z ⟧),
pr1 h · g = pr1 h · h0 → g = h0
y: C / x
f, g: C / x ⟦ b, y ⟧
eq: h · f = h · g
pr1 (h · f) = pr1 (h · g)

  
C: category
x: C
a, b: C / x
h: C / x ⟦ a, b ⟧
epich: ∏ (z : C) (g h0 : C ⟦ pr1 b, z ⟧),
pr1 h · g = pr1 h · h0 → g = h0
y: C / x
f, g: C / x ⟦ b, y ⟧
eq: h · f = h · g
h · f = h · g

  assumption.
Qed.

  (identity (pr1 Y))

    (identity x) (pr1 F)

 rewrite <- assoc, BinProductPr1Commutes, id_right, (pr2 F); apply idpath.

C: category
x: C
BPC: BinProducts C
form_adjunction slicecat_to_cat (cat_to_slicecat BPC)
  (make_nat_trans (functor_identity (C / x))
     (slicecat_to_cat ∙ cat_to_slicecat BPC)
     (((λ F : slice_precat_ob_mor C x,
        BinProductArrow C
          (BPC x
             ((pr1,, (λ a b : slicecat_ob C x, pr1)) F))
          (pr2 F) (identity (pr1 F)),,
        (is_left_adjoint_slicecat_to_cat_subproof BPC
           F
         :
         pr2
           (functor_identity_data
              (slice_precat_data C x) F) =
         BinProductArrow C
           (BPC x
              ((pr1,, (λ a b : slicecat_ob C x, pr1))
                 F)) (pr2 F) (identity (pr1 F))
         · pr2
             (functor_composite_data
                (pr1,, (λ a b : slicecat_ob C x, pr1))
                (cat_to_slicecat_data BPC) F)))
       :
       nat_trans_data
         (functor_identity_data
            (slice_precat_data C x))
         (functor_composite_data
            (pr1,, (λ a b : slicecat_ob C x, pr1))
            (cat_to_slicecat_data BPC)))
      :
      nat_trans_data (functor_identity (C / x))
        (slicecat_to_cat ∙ cat_to_slicecat BPC))
     ((λ (Y Z : C / x) (F : C / x ⟦ Y, Z ⟧),
       eq_mor_slicecat (functor_identity (C / x) Y)
         ((slicecat_to_cat ∙ cat_to_slicecat BPC) Z)
         (# (functor_identity (C / x)) F
          · (BinProductArrow C
               (BPC x
                  ((pr1,,
                    (λ a b : slicecat_ob C x, pr1)) Z))
               (pr2 Z) (identity (pr1 Z)),,
             is_left_adjoint_slicecat_to_cat_subproof
               BPC Z))
         ((BinProductArrow C
             (BPC x
                ((pr1,, (λ a b : slicecat_ob C x, pr1))
                   Y)) (pr2 Y) (identity (pr1 Y)),,
           is_left_adjoint_slicecat_to_cat_subproof
             BPC Y)
          · # (slicecat_to_cat ∙ cat_to_slicecat BPC)
              F)
         (internal_paths_rew_r
            (C ⟦ pr1 Y, BPC x (pr1 Z) ⟧)
            (BinProductArrow C (BPC x (pr1 Y)) (pr2 Y)
               (identity (pr1 Y))
             · BinProductOfArrows C (BPC x (pr1 Z))
                 (BPC x (pr1 Y)) (identity x) (pr1 F))
            (BinProductArrow C (BPC x (pr1 Z))
               (pr2 Y · identity x)
               (identity (pr1 Y) · pr1 F))
            (λ p : C ⟦ pr1 Y, BPC x (pr1 Z) ⟧,
             pr1 F
             · BinProductArrow C (BPC x (pr1 Z))
                 (pr2 Z) (identity (pr1 Z)) = p)
            (BinProductArrowUnique C x (pr1 Z)
               (BPC x (pr1 Z)) (pr1 Y)
               (pr2 Y · identity x)
               (identity (pr1 Y) · pr1 F)
               (pr1 F
                · BinProductArrow C (BPC x (pr1 Z))
                    (pr2 Z) (identity (pr1 Z)))
               (internal_paths_rew (C ⟦ pr1 Y, x ⟧)
                  (pr1 F
                   · (BinProductArrow C
                        (BPC x (pr1 Z)) (pr2 Z)
                        (identity (pr1 Z))
                      · BinProductPr1 C
                          (BPC x (pr1 Z))))
                  (λ p : C ⟦ pr1 Y, x ⟧,
                   p = pr2 Y · identity x)
                  (internal_paths_rew_r
                     (C ⟦ pr1 Z, x ⟧)
                     (BinProductArrow C
                        (BPC x (pr1 Z)) (pr2 Z)
                        (identity (pr1 Z))
                      · BinProductPr1 C
                          (BPC x (pr1 Z))) (pr2 Z)
                     (λ p : C ⟦ pr1 Z, x ⟧,
                      pr1 F · p = pr2 Y · identity x)
                     (internal_paths_rew_r
                        (C ⟦ pr1 Y, x ⟧)
                        (pr2 Y · identity x) (pr2 Y)
                        (λ p : C ⟦ pr1 Y, x ⟧,
                         pr1 F · pr2 Z = p)
                        (internal_paths_rew_r
                           (C ⟦ pr1 Y, x ⟧) (pr2 Y)
                           (pr1 F · pr2 Z)
                           (λ p : C ⟦ pr1 Y, x ⟧,
                            pr1 F · pr2 Z = p)
                           (idpath (pr1 F · pr2 Z))
                           (pr2 F)) (id_right (pr2 Y)))
                     (BinProductPr1Commutes C x
                        (pr1 Z) (BPC x (pr1 Z))
                        (pr1 Z) (pr2 Z)
                        (identity (pr1 Z))))
                  (pr1 F
                   · BinProductArrow C (BPC x (pr1 Z))
                       (pr2 Z) (identity (pr1 Z))
                   · BinProductPr1 C (BPC x (pr1 Z)))
                  (assoc (pr1 F)
                     (BinProductArrow C
                        (BPC x (pr1 Z)) (pr2 Z)
                        (identity (pr1 Z)))
                     (BinProductPr1 C (BPC x (pr1 Z)))))
               (internal_paths_rew
                  (C ⟦ pr1 Y, pr1 Z ⟧)
                  (pr1 F
                   · (BinProductArrow C
                        (BPC x (pr1 Z)) (pr2 Z)
                        (identity (pr1 Z))
                      · BinProductPr2 C
                          (BPC x (pr1 Z))))
                  (λ p : C ⟦ pr1 Y, pr1 Z ⟧,
                   p = identity (pr1 Y) · pr1 F)
                  (internal_paths_rew_r
                     (C ⟦ pr1 Z, pr1 Z ⟧)
                     (BinProductArrow C
                        (BPC x (pr1 Z)) (pr2 Z)
                        (identity (pr1 Z))
                      · BinProductPr2 C
                          (BPC x (pr1 Z)))
                     (identity (pr1 Z))
                     (λ p : C ⟦ pr1 Z, pr1 Z ⟧,
                      pr1 F · p =
                      identity (pr1 Y) · pr1 F)
                     (internal_paths_rew_r
                        (C ⟦ pr1 Y, pr1 Z ⟧)
                        (identity (pr1 Y) · pr1 F)
                        (pr1 F)
                        (λ p : C ⟦ pr1 Y, pr1 Z ⟧,
                         pr1 F · identity (pr1 Z) = p)
                        (internal_paths_rew_r
                           (C ⟦ pr1 Y, pr1 Z ⟧)
                           (pr1 F · identity (pr1 Z))
                           (pr1 F)
                           (λ p : C ⟦ pr1 Y, pr1 Z ⟧,
                            p = pr1 F)
                           (idpath (pr1 F))
                           (id_right (pr1 F)))
                        (id_left (pr1 F)))
                     (BinProductPr2Commutes C x
                        (pr1 Z) (BPC x (pr1 Z))
                        (pr1 Z) (pr2 Z)
                        (identity (pr1 Z))))
                  (pr1 F
                   · BinProductArrow C (BPC x (pr1 Z))
                       (pr2 Z) (identity (pr1 Z))
                   · BinProductPr2 C (BPC x (pr1 Z)))
                  (assoc (pr1 F)
                     (BinProductArrow C
                        (BPC x (pr1 Z)) (pr2 Z)
                        (identity (pr1 Z)))
                     (BinProductPr2 C (BPC x (pr1 Z))))))
            (postcompWithBinProductArrow C
               (BPC x (pr1 Z)) (BPC x (pr1 Y))
               (identity x) (pr1 F) (pr2 Y)
               (identity (pr1 Y)))
          :
          pr1
            (# (functor_identity (C / x)) F
             · (BinProductArrow C
                  (BPC x
                     ((pr1,,
                       (λ a b : slicecat_ob C x, pr1))
                        Z)) (pr2 Z) (identity (pr1 Z)),,
                is_left_adjoint_slicecat_to_cat_subproof
                  BPC Z)) =
          pr1
            ((BinProductArrow C
                (BPC x
                   ((pr1,,
                     (λ a b : slicecat_ob C x, pr1)) Y))
                (pr2 Y) (identity (pr1 Y)),,
              is_left_adjoint_slicecat_to_cat_subproof
                BPC Y)
             · # (slicecat_to_cat
                  ∙ cat_to_slicecat BPC) F)))
      :
      is_nat_trans (functor_identity (C / x))
        (slicecat_to_cat ∙ cat_to_slicecat BPC)
        (((λ F : slice_precat_ob_mor C x,
           BinProductArrow C
             (BPC x
                ((pr1,, (λ a b : slicecat_ob C x, pr1))
                   F)) (pr2 F) (identity (pr1 F)),,
           (is_left_adjoint_slicecat_to_cat_subproof
              BPC F
            :
            pr2
              (functor_identity_data
                 (slice_precat_data C x) F) =
            BinProductArrow C
              (BPC x ((pr1,, (λ a b : ..., pr1)) F))
              (pr2 F) (identity (pr1 F))
            · pr2
                (functor_composite_data
                   (pr1,,
                    (λ a b : slicecat_ob C x, pr1))
                   (cat_to_slicecat_data BPC) F)))
          :
          nat_trans_data
            (functor_identity_data
               (slice_precat_data C x))
            (functor_composite_data
               (pr1,, (λ a b : slicecat_ob C x, pr1))
               (cat_to_slicecat_data BPC)))
         :
         nat_trans_data (functor_identity (C / x))
           (slicecat_to_cat ∙ cat_to_slicecat BPC))))
  (make_nat_trans
     (cat_to_slicecat BPC ∙ slicecat_to_cat)
     (functor_identity C)
     ((λ Y : C, BinProductPr2 C (BPC x Y))
      :
      nat_trans_data
        (cat_to_slicecat BPC ∙ slicecat_to_cat)
        (functor_identity C))
     (is_left_adjoint_slicecat_to_cat_subproof0 BPC))
 
C: category
x: C
BPC: BinProducts C
triangle_1_statement
  (slicecat_to_cat,,
   cat_to_slicecat BPC,,
   make_nat_trans (functor_identity (C / x))
     (slicecat_to_cat ∙ cat_to_slicecat BPC)
     (λ F : slice_precat_ob_mor C x,
      BinProductArrow C
        (BPC x
           ((pr1,, (λ a b : slicecat_ob C x, pr1)) F))
        (pr2 F) (identity (pr1 F)),,
      is_left_adjoint_slicecat_to_cat_subproof BPC F)
     (λ (Y Z : C / x) (F : C / x ⟦ Y, Z ⟧),
      eq_mor_slicecat (functor_identity (C / x) Y)
        ((slicecat_to_cat ∙ cat_to_slicecat BPC) Z)
        (# (functor_identity (C / x)) F
         · (BinProductArrow C
              (BPC x
                 ((pr1,,
                   (λ a b : slicecat_ob C x, pr1)) Z))
              (pr2 Z) (identity (pr1 Z)),,
            is_left_adjoint_slicecat_to_cat_subproof
              BPC Z))
        ((BinProductArrow C
            (BPC x
               ((pr1,, (λ a b : slicecat_ob C x, pr1))
                  Y)) (pr2 Y) (identity (pr1 Y)),,
          is_left_adjoint_slicecat_to_cat_subproof BPC
            Y)
         · # (slicecat_to_cat ∙ cat_to_slicecat BPC) F)
        (internal_paths_rew_r
           (C ⟦ pr1 Y, BPC x (pr1 Z) ⟧)
           (BinProductArrow C (BPC x (pr1 Y)) (pr2 Y)
              (identity (pr1 Y))
            · BinProductOfArrows C (BPC x (pr1 Z))
                (BPC x (pr1 Y)) (identity x) (pr1 F))
           (BinProductArrow C (BPC x (pr1 Z))
              (pr2 Y · identity x)
              (identity (pr1 Y) · pr1 F))
           (λ p : C ⟦ pr1 Y, BPC x (pr1 Z) ⟧,
            pr1 F
            · BinProductArrow C (BPC x (pr1 Z))
                (pr2 Z) (identity (pr1 Z)) = p)
           (BinProductArrowUnique C x (pr1 Z)
              (BPC x (pr1 Z)) (pr1 Y)
              (pr2 Y · identity x)
              (identity (pr1 Y) · pr1 F)
              (pr1 F
               · BinProductArrow C (BPC x (pr1 Z))
                   (pr2 Z) (identity (pr1 Z)))
              (internal_paths_rew (C ⟦ pr1 Y, x ⟧)
                 (pr1 F
                  · (BinProductArrow C (BPC x (pr1 Z))
                       (pr2 Z) (identity (pr1 Z))
                     · BinProductPr1 C (BPC x (pr1 Z))))
                 (λ p : C ⟦ pr1 Y, x ⟧,
                  p = pr2 Y · identity x)
                 (internal_paths_rew_r
                    (C ⟦ pr1 Z, x ⟧)
                    (BinProductArrow C (BPC x (pr1 Z))
                       (pr2 Z) (identity (pr1 Z))
                     · BinProductPr1 C (BPC x (pr1 Z)))
                    (pr2 Z)
                    (λ p : C ⟦ pr1 Z, x ⟧,
                     pr1 F · p = pr2 Y · identity x)
                    (internal_paths_rew_r
                       (C ⟦ pr1 Y, x ⟧)
                       (pr2 Y · identity x) (pr2 Y)
                       (λ p : C ⟦ pr1 Y, x ⟧,
                        pr1 F · pr2 Z = p)
                       (internal_paths_rew_r
                          (C ⟦ pr1 Y, x ⟧) (pr2 Y)
                          (pr1 F · pr2 Z)
                          (λ p : C ⟦ pr1 Y, x ⟧,
                           pr1 F · pr2 Z = p)
                          (idpath (pr1 F · pr2 Z))
                          (pr2 F)) (id_right (pr2 Y)))
                    (BinProductPr1Commutes C x (pr1 Z)
                       (BPC x (pr1 Z)) (pr1 Z) (pr2 Z)
                       (identity (pr1 Z))))
                 (pr1 F
                  · BinProductArrow C (BPC x (pr1 Z))
                      (pr2 Z) (identity (pr1 Z))
                  · BinProductPr1 C (BPC x (pr1 Z)))
                 (assoc (pr1 F)
                    (BinProductArrow C (BPC x (pr1 Z))
                       (pr2 Z) (identity (pr1 Z)))
                    (BinProductPr1 C (BPC x (pr1 Z)))))
              (internal_paths_rew (C ⟦ pr1 Y, pr1 Z ⟧)
                 (pr1 F
                  · (BinProductArrow C (BPC x (pr1 Z))
                       (pr2 Z) (identity (pr1 Z))
                     · BinProductPr2 C (BPC x (pr1 Z))))
                 (λ p : C ⟦ pr1 Y, pr1 Z ⟧,
                  p = identity (pr1 Y) · pr1 F)
                 (internal_paths_rew_r
                    (C ⟦ pr1 Z, pr1 Z ⟧)
                    (BinProductArrow C (BPC x (pr1 Z))
                       (pr2 Z) (identity (pr1 Z))
                     · BinProductPr2 C (BPC x (pr1 Z)))
                    (identity (pr1 Z))
                    (λ p : C ⟦ pr1 Z, pr1 Z ⟧,
                     pr1 F · p =
                     identity (pr1 Y) · pr1 F)
                    (internal_paths_rew_r
                       (C ⟦ pr1 Y, pr1 Z ⟧)
                       (identity (pr1 Y) · pr1 F)
                       (pr1 F)
                       (λ p : C ⟦ pr1 Y, pr1 Z ⟧,
                        pr1 F · identity (pr1 Z) = p)
                       (internal_paths_rew_r
                          (C ⟦ pr1 Y, pr1 Z ⟧)
                          (pr1 F · identity (pr1 Z))
                          (pr1 F)
                          (λ p : C ⟦ pr1 Y, pr1 Z ⟧,
                           p = pr1 F) (idpath (pr1 F))
                          (id_right (pr1 F)))
                       (id_left (pr1 F)))
                    (BinProductPr2Commutes C x (pr1 Z)
                       (BPC x (pr1 Z)) (pr1 Z) (pr2 Z)
                       (identity (pr1 Z))))
                 (pr1 F
                  · BinProductArrow C (BPC x (pr1 Z))
                      (pr2 Z) (identity (pr1 Z))
                  · BinProductPr2 C (BPC x (pr1 Z)))
                 (assoc (pr1 F)
                    (BinProductArrow C (BPC x (pr1 Z))
                       (pr2 Z) (identity (pr1 Z)))
                    (BinProductPr2 C (BPC x (pr1 Z))))))
           (postcompWithBinProductArrow C
              (BPC x (pr1 Z)) (BPC x (pr1 Y))
              (identity x) (pr1 F) (pr2 Y)
              (identity (pr1 Y))))),,
   make_nat_trans
     (cat_to_slicecat BPC ∙ slicecat_to_cat)
     (functor_identity C)
     (λ Y : C, BinProductPr2 C (BPC x Y))
     (is_left_adjoint_slicecat_to_cat_subproof0 BPC))
C: category
x: C
BPC: BinProducts C
triangle_2_statement
  (slicecat_to_cat,,
   cat_to_slicecat BPC,,
   make_nat_trans (functor_identity (C / x))
     (slicecat_to_cat ∙ cat_to_slicecat BPC)
     (λ F : slice_precat_ob_mor C x,
      BinProductArrow C
        (BPC x
           ((pr1,, (λ a b : slicecat_ob C x, pr1)) F))
        (pr2 F) (identity (pr1 F)),,
      is_left_adjoint_slicecat_to_cat_subproof BPC F)
     (λ (Y Z : C / x) (F : C / x ⟦ Y, Z ⟧),
      eq_mor_slicecat (functor_identity (C / x) Y)
        ((slicecat_to_cat ∙ cat_to_slicecat BPC) Z)
        (# (functor_identity (C / x)) F
         · (BinProductArrow C
              (BPC x
                 ((pr1,,
                   (λ a b : slicecat_ob C x, pr1)) Z))
              (pr2 Z) (identity (pr1 Z)),,
            is_left_adjoint_slicecat_to_cat_subproof
              BPC Z))
        ((BinProductArrow C
            (BPC x
               ((pr1,, (λ a b : slicecat_ob C x, pr1))
                  Y)) (pr2 Y) (identity (pr1 Y)),,
          is_left_adjoint_slicecat_to_cat_subproof BPC
            Y)
         · # (slicecat_to_cat ∙ cat_to_slicecat BPC) F)
        (internal_paths_rew_r
           (C ⟦ pr1 Y, BPC x (pr1 Z) ⟧)
           (BinProductArrow C (BPC x (pr1 Y)) (pr2 Y)
              (identity (pr1 Y))
            · BinProductOfArrows C (BPC x (pr1 Z))
                (BPC x (pr1 Y)) (identity x) (pr1 F))
           (BinProductArrow C (BPC x (pr1 Z))
              (pr2 Y · identity x)
              (identity (pr1 Y) · pr1 F))
           (λ p : C ⟦ pr1 Y, BPC x (pr1 Z) ⟧,
            pr1 F
            · BinProductArrow C (BPC x (pr1 Z))
                (pr2 Z) (identity (pr1 Z)) = p)
           (BinProductArrowUnique C x (pr1 Z)
              (BPC x (pr1 Z)) (pr1 Y)
              (pr2 Y · identity x)
              (identity (pr1 Y) · pr1 F)
              (pr1 F
               · BinProductArrow C (BPC x (pr1 Z))
                   (pr2 Z) (identity (pr1 Z)))
              (internal_paths_rew (C ⟦ pr1 Y, x ⟧)
                 (pr1 F
                  · (BinProductArrow C (BPC x (pr1 Z))
                       (pr2 Z) (identity (pr1 Z))
                     · BinProductPr1 C (BPC x (pr1 Z))))
                 (λ p : C ⟦ pr1 Y, x ⟧,
                  p = pr2 Y · identity x)
                 (internal_paths_rew_r
                    (C ⟦ pr1 Z, x ⟧)
                    (BinProductArrow C (BPC x (pr1 Z))
                       (pr2 Z) (identity (pr1 Z))
                     · BinProductPr1 C (BPC x (pr1 Z)))
                    (pr2 Z)
                    (λ p : C ⟦ pr1 Z, x ⟧,
                     pr1 F · p = pr2 Y · identity x)
                    (internal_paths_rew_r
                       (C ⟦ pr1 Y, x ⟧)
                       (pr2 Y · identity x) (pr2 Y)
                       (λ p : C ⟦ pr1 Y, x ⟧,
                        pr1 F · pr2 Z = p)
                       (internal_paths_rew_r
                          (C ⟦ pr1 Y, x ⟧) (pr2 Y)
                          (pr1 F · pr2 Z)
                          (λ p : C ⟦ pr1 Y, x ⟧,
                           pr1 F · pr2 Z = p)
                          (idpath (pr1 F · pr2 Z))
                          (pr2 F)) (id_right (pr2 Y)))
                    (BinProductPr1Commutes C x (pr1 Z)
                       (BPC x (pr1 Z)) (pr1 Z) (pr2 Z)
                       (identity (pr1 Z))))
                 (pr1 F
                  · BinProductArrow C (BPC x (pr1 Z))
                      (pr2 Z) (identity (pr1 Z))
                  · BinProductPr1 C (BPC x (pr1 Z)))
                 (assoc (pr1 F)
                    (BinProductArrow C (BPC x (pr1 Z))
                       (pr2 Z) (identity (pr1 Z)))
                    (BinProductPr1 C (BPC x (pr1 Z)))))
              (internal_paths_rew (C ⟦ pr1 Y, pr1 Z ⟧)
                 (pr1 F
                  · (BinProductArrow C (BPC x (pr1 Z))
                       (pr2 Z) (identity (pr1 Z))
                     · BinProductPr2 C (BPC x (pr1 Z))))
                 (λ p : C ⟦ pr1 Y, pr1 Z ⟧,
                  p = identity (pr1 Y) · pr1 F)
                 (internal_paths_rew_r
                    (C ⟦ pr1 Z, pr1 Z ⟧)
                    (BinProductArrow C (BPC x (pr1 Z))
                       (pr2 Z) (identity (pr1 Z))
                     · BinProductPr2 C (BPC x (pr1 Z)))
                    (identity (pr1 Z))
                    (λ p : C ⟦ pr1 Z, pr1 Z ⟧,
                     pr1 F · p =
                     identity (pr1 Y) · pr1 F)
                    (internal_paths_rew_r
                       (C ⟦ pr1 Y, pr1 Z ⟧)
                       (identity (pr1 Y) · pr1 F)
                       (pr1 F)
                       (λ p : C ⟦ pr1 Y, pr1 Z ⟧,
                        pr1 F · identity (pr1 Z) = p)
                       (internal_paths_rew_r
                          (C ⟦ pr1 Y, pr1 Z ⟧)
                          (pr1 F · identity (pr1 Z))
                          (pr1 F)
                          (λ p : C ⟦ pr1 Y, pr1 Z ⟧,
                           p = pr1 F) (idpath (pr1 F))
                          (id_right (pr1 F)))
                       (id_left (pr1 F)))
                    (BinProductPr2Commutes C x (pr1 Z)
                       (BPC x (pr1 Z)) (pr1 Z) (pr2 Z)
                       (identity (pr1 Z))))
                 (pr1 F
                  · BinProductArrow C (BPC x (pr1 Z))
                      (pr2 Z) (identity (pr1 Z))
                  · BinProductPr2 C (BPC x (pr1 Z)))
                 (assoc (pr1 F)
                    (BinProductArrow C (BPC x (pr1 Z))
                       (pr2 Z) (identity (pr1 Z)))
                    (BinProductPr2 C (BPC x (pr1 Z))))))
           (postcompWithBinProductArrow C
              (BPC x (pr1 Z)) (BPC x (pr1 Y))
              (identity x) (pr1 F) (pr2 Y)
              (identity (pr1 Y))))),,
   make_nat_trans
     (cat_to_slicecat BPC ∙ slicecat_to_cat)
     (functor_identity C)
     (λ Y : C, BinProductPr2 C (BPC x Y))
     (is_left_adjoint_slicecat_to_cat_subproof0 BPC))

  
C: category
x: C
BPC: BinProducts C
triangle_1_statement
  (slicecat_to_cat,,
   cat_to_slicecat BPC,,
   make_nat_trans (functor_identity (C / x))
     (slicecat_to_cat ∙ cat_to_slicecat BPC)
     (λ F : slice_precat_ob_mor C x,
      BinProductArrow C
        (BPC x
           ((pr1,, (λ a b : slicecat_ob C x, pr1)) F))
        (pr2 F) (identity (pr1 F)),,
      is_left_adjoint_slicecat_to_cat_subproof BPC F)
     (λ (Y Z : C / x) (F : C / x ⟦ Y, Z ⟧),
      eq_mor_slicecat (functor_identity (C / x) Y)
        ((slicecat_to_cat ∙ cat_to_slicecat BPC) Z)
        (# (functor_identity (C / x)) F
         · (BinProductArrow C
              (BPC x
                 ((pr1,,
                   (λ a b : slicecat_ob C x, pr1)) Z))
              (pr2 Z) (identity (pr1 Z)),,
            is_left_adjoint_slicecat_to_cat_subproof
              BPC Z))
        ((BinProductArrow C
            (BPC x
               ((pr1,, (λ a b : slicecat_ob C x, pr1))
                  Y)) (pr2 Y) (identity (pr1 Y)),,
          is_left_adjoint_slicecat_to_cat_subproof BPC
            Y)
         · # (slicecat_to_cat ∙ cat_to_slicecat BPC) F)
        (internal_paths_rew_r
           (C ⟦ pr1 Y, BPC x (pr1 Z) ⟧)
           (BinProductArrow C (BPC x (pr1 Y)) (pr2 Y)
              (identity (pr1 Y))
            · BinProductOfArrows C (BPC x (pr1 Z))
                (BPC x (pr1 Y)) (identity x) (pr1 F))
           (BinProductArrow C (BPC x (pr1 Z))
              (pr2 Y · identity x)
              (identity (pr1 Y) · pr1 F))
           (λ p : C ⟦ pr1 Y, BPC x (pr1 Z) ⟧,
            pr1 F
            · BinProductArrow C (BPC x (pr1 Z))
                (pr2 Z) (identity (pr1 Z)) = p)
           (BinProductArrowUnique C x (pr1 Z)
              (BPC x (pr1 Z)) (pr1 Y)
              (pr2 Y · identity x)
              (identity (pr1 Y) · pr1 F)
              (pr1 F
               · BinProductArrow C (BPC x (pr1 Z))
                   (pr2 Z) (identity (pr1 Z)))
              (internal_paths_rew (C ⟦ pr1 Y, x ⟧)
                 (pr1 F
                  · (BinProductArrow C (BPC x (pr1 Z))
                       (pr2 Z) (identity (pr1 Z))
                     · BinProductPr1 C (BPC x (pr1 Z))))
                 (λ p : C ⟦ pr1 Y, x ⟧,
                  p = pr2 Y · identity x)
                 (internal_paths_rew_r
                    (C ⟦ pr1 Z, x ⟧)
                    (BinProductArrow C (BPC x (pr1 Z))
                       (pr2 Z) (identity (pr1 Z))
                     · BinProductPr1 C (BPC x (pr1 Z)))
                    (pr2 Z)
                    (λ p : C ⟦ pr1 Z, x ⟧,
                     pr1 F · p = pr2 Y · identity x)
                    (internal_paths_rew_r
                       (C ⟦ pr1 Y, x ⟧)
                       (pr2 Y · identity x) (pr2 Y)
                       (λ p : C ⟦ pr1 Y, x ⟧,
                        pr1 F · pr2 Z = p)
                       (internal_paths_rew_r
                          (C ⟦ pr1 Y, x ⟧) (pr2 Y)
                          (pr1 F · pr2 Z)
                          (λ p : C ⟦ pr1 Y, x ⟧,
                           pr1 F · pr2 Z = p)
                          (idpath (pr1 F · pr2 Z))
                          (pr2 F)) (id_right (pr2 Y)))
                    (BinProductPr1Commutes C x (pr1 Z)
                       (BPC x (pr1 Z)) (pr1 Z) (pr2 Z)
                       (identity (pr1 Z))))
                 (pr1 F
                  · BinProductArrow C (BPC x (pr1 Z))
                      (pr2 Z) (identity (pr1 Z))
                  · BinProductPr1 C (BPC x (pr1 Z)))
                 (assoc (pr1 F)
                    (BinProductArrow C (BPC x (pr1 Z))
                       (pr2 Z) (identity (pr1 Z)))
                    (BinProductPr1 C (BPC x (pr1 Z)))))
              (internal_paths_rew (C ⟦ pr1 Y, pr1 Z ⟧)
                 (pr1 F
                  · (BinProductArrow C (BPC x (pr1 Z))
                       (pr2 Z) (identity (pr1 Z))
                     · BinProductPr2 C (BPC x (pr1 Z))))
                 (λ p : C ⟦ pr1 Y, pr1 Z ⟧,
                  p = identity (pr1 Y) · pr1 F)
                 (internal_paths_rew_r
                    (C ⟦ pr1 Z, pr1 Z ⟧)
                    (BinProductArrow C (BPC x (pr1 Z))
                       (pr2 Z) (identity (pr1 Z))
                     · BinProductPr2 C (BPC x (pr1 Z)))
                    (identity (pr1 Z))
                    (λ p : C ⟦ pr1 Z, pr1 Z ⟧,
                     pr1 F · p =
                     identity (pr1 Y) · pr1 F)
                    (internal_paths_rew_r
                       (C ⟦ pr1 Y, pr1 Z ⟧)
                       (identity (pr1 Y) · pr1 F)
                       (pr1 F)
                       (λ p : C ⟦ pr1 Y, pr1 Z ⟧,
                        pr1 F · identity (pr1 Z) = p)
                       (internal_paths_rew_r
                          (C ⟦ pr1 Y, pr1 Z ⟧)
                          (pr1 F · identity (pr1 Z))
                          (pr1 F)
                          (λ p : C ⟦ pr1 Y, pr1 Z ⟧,
                           p = pr1 F) (idpath (pr1 F))
                          (id_right (pr1 F)))
                       (id_left (pr1 F)))
                    (BinProductPr2Commutes C x (pr1 Z)
                       (BPC x (pr1 Z)) (pr1 Z) (pr2 Z)
                       (identity (pr1 Z))))
                 (pr1 F
                  · BinProductArrow C (BPC x (pr1 Z))
                      (pr2 Z) (identity (pr1 Z))
                  · BinProductPr2 C (BPC x (pr1 Z)))
                 (assoc (pr1 F)
                    (BinProductArrow C (BPC x (pr1 Z))
                       (pr2 Z) (identity (pr1 Z)))
                    (BinProductPr2 C (BPC x (pr1 Z))))))
           (postcompWithBinProductArrow C
              (BPC x (pr1 Z)) (BPC x (pr1 Y))
              (identity x) (pr1 F) (pr2 Y)
              (identity (pr1 Y))))),,
   make_nat_trans
     (cat_to_slicecat BPC ∙ slicecat_to_cat)
     (functor_identity C)
     (λ Y : C, BinProductPr2 C (BPC x Y))
     (is_left_adjoint_slicecat_to_cat_subproof0 BPC))
 
C: category
x: C
BPC: BinProducts C
Y: C / x
BinProductArrow C (BPC x (pr1 Y)) (pr2 Y)
  (identity (pr1 Y)) · BinProductPr2 C (BPC x (pr1 Y)) =
identity (pr1 Y)

    rewrite BinProductPr2Commutes; apply idpath.

C: category
x: C
BPC: BinProducts C
Y: C
BinProductArrow C (BPC x (BPC x Y))
  (BinProductPr1 C (BPC x Y)) (identity (BPC x Y))
· BinProductOfArrows C (BPC x Y) (BPC x (BPC x Y))
    (identity x) (BinProductPr2 C (BPC x Y)) =
identity (BPC x Y)

    
C: category
x: C
BPC: BinProducts C
Y: C
BinProductArrow C (BPC x Y)
  (BinProductPr1 C (BPC x Y) · identity x)
  (identity (BPC x Y) · BinProductPr2 C (BPC x Y)) =
identity (BPC x Y)

    
C: category
x: C
BPC: BinProducts C
Y: C
identity (BPC x Y) · BinProductPr1 C (BPC x Y) =
BinProductPr1 C (BPC x Y) · identity x

    rewrite id_right, id_left; apply idpath.
Defined.
(* it would be better if the preceding def. had much larger opaque parts *)

End slice_precat_theory.

End slicecat_theory.

(** * A morphism x --> y in the base category induces a functor between C/x and C/y *)
Section slicecat_functor_def.

Context {C : category} {x y : C} (f : C⟦x,y⟧).

Local Notation "C / X" := (slice_cat C X).

Definition slicecat_functor_ob (af : C / x) : C / y :=
  (pr1 af,,pr2 af · f).


C: category
x, y: C
f: C ⟦ x, y ⟧
af, bg: C / x
h: C / x ⟦ af, bg ⟧
pr2 af · f = pr1 h · (pr2 bg · f)


C: category
x, y: C
f: C ⟦ x, y ⟧
af, bg: C / x
h: C / x ⟦ af, bg ⟧
pr2 af · f = pr1 h · (pr2 bg · f)

rewrite assoc, <- (pr2 h); apply idpath.
Qed.

Definition slicecat_functor_data : functor_data (C / x) (C / y) :=
  tpair (λ F, ∏ a b, C/x⟦a,b⟧ → C/y⟦F a,F b⟧) slicecat_functor_ob
        (λ a b h, (pr1 h,,slicecat_functor_subproof _ _ h)).


C: category
x, y: C
f: C ⟦ x, y ⟧
is_functor slicecat_functor_data


C: category
x, y: C
f: C ⟦ x, y ⟧
is_functor slicecat_functor_data


C: category
x, y: C
f: C ⟦ x, y ⟧
functor_idax slicecat_functor_data
C: category
x, y: C
f: C ⟦ x, y ⟧
functor_compax slicecat_functor_data


C: category
x, y: C
f: C ⟦ x, y ⟧
functor_idax slicecat_functor_data
 intros a; apply eq_mor_slicecat, idpath.

C: category
x, y: C
f: C ⟦ x, y ⟧
functor_compax slicecat_functor_data
 intros a b c g h; apply eq_mor_slicecat, idpath.
Qed.

Definition slicecat_functor : functor (C / x) (C / y) :=
  (slicecat_functor_data,,is_functor_slicecat_functor).

End slicecat_functor_def.

Section slicecat_functor_theory.

Context (C : category).

Local Notation "C / X" := (slice_precat C X).


C: category
x: C
slicecat_functor_ob (identity x) =
functor_identity (C / x)


C: category
x: C
slicecat_functor_ob (identity x) =
functor_identity (C / x)


C: category
x: C
af: slice_cat C x
slicecat_functor_ob (identity x) af =
functor_identity (C / x) af


C: category
x: C
af: slice_cat C x
pr1 af,, pr2 af · identity x =
functor_identity (C / x) af


C: category
x: C
af: slice_cat C x
pr1 af,, pr2 af = functor_identity (C / x) af

apply idpath.
Defined.


C: category
x: C
slicecat_functor (identity x) =
functor_identity (C / x)


C: category
x: C
slicecat_functor (identity x) =
functor_identity (C / x)

  
C: category
x: C
slicecat_functor_data (identity x) =
functor_identity_data (slice_precat_data C x)

  
C: category
x: C
transportf
  (λ F : slice_cat C x → slice_cat C x,
   ∏ a b : slice_cat C x,
   slice_cat C x ⟦ a, b ⟧ → slice_cat C x ⟦ F a, F b ⟧)
  (slicecat_functor_identity_ob x)
  (λ (a b : slice_cat C x)
   (h : slice_cat C x ⟦ a, b ⟧),
   pr1 h,,
   slicecat_functor_subproof (identity x) a b h) =
(λ (a b : slice_precat_data C x)
 (f : slice_precat_data C x ⟦ a, b ⟧), f)

  
C: category
x, a: C
f: C ⟦ a, x ⟧
transportf
  (λ F : slice_cat C x → slice_cat C x,
   ∏ a b : slice_cat C x,
   slice_cat C x ⟦ a, b ⟧ → slice_cat C x ⟦ F a, F b ⟧)
  (slicecat_functor_identity_ob x)
  (λ (a b : slice_cat C x)
   (h : slice_cat C x ⟦ a, b ⟧),
   pr1 h,,
   slicecat_functor_subproof (identity x) a b h)
  (a,, f) =
(λ (b : slice_precat_data C x)
 (f : slice_precat_data C x ⟦ a,, f, b ⟧), f)

   slicecat_functor_subproof (identity x) a b h)
  (a,, f) (b,, g) =

C: category

transportf (λ x : slicecat_ob C x, C ⟦ a, pr1 x ⟧)
  (toforallpaths
     (λ _ : slicecat_ob C x, slicecat_ob C x)
     (slicecat_functor_ob (identity x))
     (λ a : slicecat_ob C x, a)
     (funextsec (λ _ : slice_cat C x, slice_cat C x)
        (slicecat_functor_ob (identity x))
        (functor_identity (C / x))
        (λ af : slice_cat C x,
         internal_paths_rew_r (C ⟦ pr1 af, x ⟧)
           (pr2 af · identity x) (pr2 af)
           (λ p : C ⟦ pr1 af, x ⟧,
            pr1 af,, p = functor_identity (C / x) af)
           (idpath (functor_identity (C / x) af))
           (id_right (pr2 af)))) (b,, g))
  (transportf (λ x : slicecat_ob C x, C ⟦ pr1 x, b ⟧)
     (toforallpaths
        (λ _ : slicecat_ob C x, slicecat_ob C x)
        (slicecat_functor_ob (identity x))
        (λ a : slicecat_ob C x, a)
        (funextsec
           (λ _ : slice_cat C x, slice_cat C x)
           (slicecat_functor_ob (identity x))
           (functor_identity (C / x))
           (λ af : slice_cat C x,
            internal_paths_rew_r (C ⟦ pr1 af, x ⟧)
              (pr2 af · identity x) (pr2 af)
              (λ p : C ⟦ pr1 af, x ⟧,
               pr1 af,, p =
               functor_identity (C / x) af)
              (idpath (functor_identity (C / x) af))
              (id_right (pr2 af)))) (a,, f)) h) = h

C: category
x, y, z: C
f: C ⟦ x, y ⟧
g: C ⟦ y, z ⟧
slicecat_functor_ob (f · g) =
(λ a : slice_cat C x,
 slicecat_functor_ob g (slicecat_functor_ob f a))


C: category
x, y, z: C
f: C ⟦ x, y ⟧
g: C ⟦ y, z ⟧
slicecat_functor_ob (f · g) =
(λ a : slice_cat C x,
 slicecat_functor_ob g (slicecat_functor_ob f a))


C: category
x, y, z: C
f: C ⟦ x, y ⟧
g: C ⟦ y, z ⟧
af: slice_cat C x
slicecat_functor_ob (f · g) af =
slicecat_functor_ob g (slicecat_functor_ob f af)

C: category

f: C ⟦ x, y ⟧
g: C ⟦ y, z ⟧
slicecat_functor (f · g) =
slicecat_functor f ∙ slicecat_functor g


C: category
x, y, z: C
f: C ⟦ x, y ⟧
g: C ⟦ y, z ⟧
slicecat_functor (f · g) =
slicecat_functor f ∙ slicecat_functor g


C: category
x, y, z: C
f: C ⟦ x, y ⟧
g: C ⟦ y, z ⟧
slicecat_functor_data (f · g) =
functor_composite_data (slicecat_functor_data f)
  (slicecat_functor_data g)


C: category
x, y, z: C
f: C ⟦ x, y ⟧
g: C ⟦ y, z ⟧
slicecat_functor_ob (f · g),,
(λ (a b : slicecat_ob C x) (h : slicecat_mor C x a b),
 pr1 h,, slicecat_functor_subproof (f · g) a b h) =
functor_composite_data
  (slicecat_functor_ob f,,
   (λ (a b : slicecat_ob C x)
    (h : slicecat_mor C x a b),
    pr1 h,, slicecat_functor_subproof f a b h))
  (slicecat_functor_ob g,,
   (λ (a b : slicecat_ob C y)
    (h : slicecat_mor C y a b),
    pr1 h,, slicecat_functor_subproof g a b h))


C: category
x, y, z: C
f: C ⟦ x, y ⟧
g: C ⟦ y, z ⟧
slicecat_functor_ob (f · g),,
(λ (a b : slicecat_ob C x) (h : slicecat_mor C x a b),
 pr1 h,, slicecat_functor_subproof (f · g) a b h) =
functor_data_constr (slice_precat_ob_mor C x)
  (slice_precat_ob_mor C z)
  (λ a : slicecat_ob C x,
   slicecat_functor_ob g (slicecat_functor_ob f a))
  (λ (a b : slicecat_ob C x)
   (f0 : slicecat_mor C x a b),
   pr1 f0,,
   slicecat_functor_subproof g
     (slicecat_functor_ob f a)
     (slicecat_functor_ob f b)
     (pr1 f0,, slicecat_functor_subproof f a b f0))


C: category

g: C ⟦ y, z ⟧
transportf
  (λ F : slicecat_ob C x → slicecat_ob C z,
   ∏ a b : slicecat_ob C x,
   slicecat_mor C x a b → slicecat_mor C z (F a) (F b))
  (slicecat_functor_comp_ob f g)
  (λ (a b : slicecat_ob C x)
   (h : slicecat_mor C x a b),
   pr1 h,, slicecat_functor_subproof (f · g) a b h) =
(λ (a b : slicecat_ob C x)
 (f0 : slicecat_mor C x a b),
 pr1 f0,,
 slicecat_functor_subproof g (slicecat_functor_ob f a)
   (slicecat_functor_ob f b)
   (pr1 f0,, slicecat_functor_subproof f a b f0))

  (λ F : slicecat_ob C x → slicecat_ob C z,

double_transport
  (toforallpaths
     (λ _ : slicecat_ob C x, slicecat_ob C z)
     (slicecat_functor_ob (f · g))
     (λ a : slicecat_ob C x,
      slicecat_functor_ob g (slicecat_functor_ob f a))
     (slicecat_functor_comp_ob f g) (a,, fax))
  (toforallpaths

     (slicecat_functor_comp_ob f g) (b,, fbx))

   slicecat_functor_subproof (f · g) (a,, fax)
     (b,, fbx) (h,, hh)) =

slicecat_functor_subproof g
  (slicecat_functor_ob f (a,, fax))
  (slicecat_functor_ob f (b,, fbx))

       (fbx · f · g)
       (λ p : (λ a : C, C ⟦ a, z ⟧) b,
        b,, p = b,, fbx · f · g)
       (idpath (b,, fbx · f · g)) (assoc fbx f g))
    h' = h
transportf (λ x : slicecat_ob C z, C ⟦ a, pr1 x ⟧)
  (internal_paths_rew_r (C ⟦ b, z ⟧) (fbx · (f · g))
     (fbx · f · g)
     (λ p : C ⟦ b, z ⟧, b,, p = b,, fbx · f · g)
     (idpath (b,, fbx · f · g)) (assoc fbx f g))
  (transportf (λ x : slicecat_ob C z, C ⟦ pr1 x, b ⟧)
     (internal_paths_rew_r (C ⟦ a, z ⟧)
        (fax · (f · g)) (fax · f · g)
        (λ p : C ⟦ a, z ⟧, a,, p = a,, fax · f · g)
        (idpath (a,, fax · f · g)) (assoc fax f g)) h) =
h

  
C: category
x, y, z: C
f: C ⟦ x, y ⟧
g: C ⟦ y, z ⟧
a: C
fax: C ⟦ a, x ⟧
b: C
fbx: C ⟦ b, x ⟧
h: C ⟦ a, b ⟧
hh: fax = h · fbx
H1: transportf (λ x : C / z, C ⟦ pr1 x, b ⟧)
  (internal_paths_rew_r ((λ a : C, C ⟦ a, z ⟧) a)
     (fax · (f · g)) (fax · f · g)
     (λ p : (λ a : C, C ⟦ a, z ⟧) a,
      a,, p = a,, fax · f · g)
     (idpath (a,, fax · f · g)) (assoc fax f g))
  h = h
H2: ∏ h' : C ⟦ a, b ⟧,
h' = h
→ transportf (λ x : C / z, C ⟦ a, pr1 x ⟧)
    (internal_paths_rew_r
       ((λ a : C, C ⟦ a, z ⟧) b) (fbx · (f · g))
       (fbx · f · g)
       (λ p : (λ a : C, C ⟦ a, z ⟧) b,
        b,, p = b,, fbx · f · g)
       (idpath (b,, fbx · f · g)) (assoc fbx f g))
    h' = h
transportf (λ x : slicecat_ob C z, C ⟦ a, pr1 x ⟧)
  (internal_paths_rew_r (C ⟦ b, z ⟧) (fbx · (f · g))
     (fbx · f · g)
     (λ p : C ⟦ b, z ⟧, b,, p = b,, fbx · f · g)
     (idpath (b,, fbx · f · g)) (assoc fbx f g))
  (transportf (λ x : slicecat_ob C z, C ⟦ pr1 x, b ⟧)
     (internal_paths_rew_r (C ⟦ a, z ⟧)
        (fax · (f · g)) (fax · f · g)
        (λ p : C ⟦ a, z ⟧, a,, p = a,, fax · f · g)
        (idpath (a,, fax · f · g)) (assoc fax f g)) h) =
h


C: category
x, y, z: C
f: C ⟦ x, y ⟧
g: C ⟦ y, z ⟧
a: C
fax: C ⟦ a, x ⟧
b: C
fbx: C ⟦ b, x ⟧
h: C ⟦ a, b ⟧
hh: fax = h · fbx
H1: transportf (λ x : C / z, C ⟦ pr1 x, b ⟧)
  (internal_paths_rew_r ((λ a : C, C ⟦ a, z ⟧) a)
     (fax · (f · g)) (fax · f · g)
     (λ p : (λ a : C, C ⟦ a, z ⟧) a,
      a,, p = a,, fax · f · g)
     (idpath (a,, fax · f · g)) (assoc fax f g))
  h = h
H2: ∏ h' : C ⟦ a, b ⟧,
h' = h
→ transportf (λ x : C / z, C ⟦ a, pr1 x ⟧)
    (internal_paths_rew_r
       ((λ a : C, C ⟦ a, z ⟧) b) (fbx · (f · g))
       (fbx · f · g)
       (λ p : (λ a : C, C ⟦ a, z ⟧) b,
        b,, p = b,, fbx · f · g)
       (idpath (b,, fbx · f · g)) (assoc fbx f g))
    h' = h
transportf (λ x : slicecat_ob C z, C ⟦ pr1 x, b ⟧)
  (internal_paths_rew_r (C ⟦ a, z ⟧) (fax · (f · g))
     (fax · f · g)
     (λ p : C ⟦ a, z ⟧, a,, p = a,, fax · f · g)
     (idpath (a,, fax · f · g)) (assoc fax f g)) h = h
 exact H1.
Qed.

End slicecat_functor_theory.

   (slice_precat_isColimCocone_subproof d a cc H y ccy
    :
    (λ h : C ⟦ pr1 a, pr1 y ⟧, pr2 a = h · pr2 y)
      (colimArrow CC (pr1 y) (mapcocone U d ccy)
       :

g: graph

→ y0 =
  (colimArrow CC (pr1 y) (mapcocone U d ccy)
   :
   C ⟦ pr1 a, pr1 y ⟧),,
  (slice_precat_isColimCocone_subproof d a cc H y ccy
   :
   (λ h : C ⟦ pr1 a, pr1 y ⟧, pr2 a = h · pr2 y)
     (colimArrow CC (pr1 y) (mapcocone U d ccy)
      :
      C ⟦ pr1 a, pr1 y ⟧))
 abstract (intros f; simpl; intros Hf;
            apply eq_mor_slicecat; simpl;
            apply (colimArrowUnique CC); intro u; cbn;
            rewrite <- (Hf u); apply idpath).
Defined.

forms_cocone d
  (λ v : vertex g,
   (colimIn H v
    :
    C ⟦ pr1 (dob d v),
    pr1
      (colim H,,
       colimArrow H x
         (make_cocone
            (λ v0 : vertex g, pr2 (dob d v0))
            (slice_precat_ColimCocone_subproof d))) ⟧),,
   (slice_precat_ColimCocone_subproof0 d H v
    :
    (λ h : C ⟦ pr1 (dob d v),
           pr1
             (colim H,,
              colimArrow H x
                (make_cocone
                   (λ v0 : vertex g, pr2 (dob d v0))
                   (slice_precat_ColimCocone_subproof
                      d))) ⟧,
     pr2 (dob d v) =
     h
     · pr2
         (colim H,,
          colimArrow H x
            (make_cocone
               (λ v0 : vertex g, pr2 (dob d v0))
               (slice_precat_ColimCocone_subproof d))))
      (colimIn H v
       :
       C ⟦ pr1 (dob d v),
       pr1
         (colim H,,
          colimArrow H x
            (make_cocone
               (λ v0 : vertex g, pr2 (dob d v0))
               (slice_precat_ColimCocone_subproof d)))
       ⟧))
   :
   C / x ⟦ dob d v,
   colim H,,
   colimArrow H x
     (make_cocone (λ v0 : vertex g, pr2 (dob d v0))
        (slice_precat_ColimCocone_subproof d)) ⟧)
 abstract (intros u v e; apply eq_mor_slicecat, (coconeInCommutes (colimCocone H))).

g: graph
C: category
x: C
U:= slicecat_to_cat C x: (C / x) ⟶ C

  (colim H,,
   colimArrow H x
     (make_cocone (λ v : vertex g, pr2 (dob d v))
        (slice_precat_ColimCocone_subproof d)))
  (make_cocone
     (λ v : vertex g,
      (colimIn H v
       :
       C ⟦ pr1 (dob d v),
       pr1
         (colim H,,
          colimArrow H x
            (make_cocone

     (slice_precat_ColimCocone_subproof1 d H))

(** * Moving between Binary products in slice categories and Pullbacks in base category *)

          PullbackPr2 P,, PullbackSqrCommutes P) ⟧,
 t
 · pr1
     (pr2
        ((P,, PullbackPr1 P · f),,
         (PullbackPr1 P,,
          idpath (pr2 (P,, PullbackPr1 P · f))),,
         PullbackPr2 P,, PullbackSqrCommutes P)) =
 j,, jeq
 × t
   · pr2
       (pr2
          ((P,, PullbackPr1 P · f),,
           (PullbackPr1 P,,
            idpath (pr2 (P,, PullbackPr1 P · f))),,
           PullbackPr2 P,, PullbackSqrCommutes P)) =
   k,, keq)
  (PullbackArrow P (pr1 Y) j k
     (pullback_to_slice_binprod_subproof A B Z f g Y j
        jeq k keq),,
   pullback_to_slice_binprod_subproof0 A B Z f g P Y j
     jeq k keq)
 abstract (split; apply eq_mor_slicecat; simpl;
              [ apply PullbackArrow_PullbackPr1 | apply PullbackArrow_PullbackPr2 ]).
  
C: category
A, B, Z: C
f: C ⟦ A, Z ⟧
g: C ⟦ B, Z ⟧
P: Pullback f g
Y: C / Z
j: C ⟦ pr1 Y, pr1 (A,, f) ⟧
jeq: pr2 Y = j · f
k: C ⟦ pr1 Y, pr1 (B,, g) ⟧
keq: pr2 Y = k · g
∏
y : C / Z ⟦ Y,
    pr1
      ((P,, PullbackPr1 P · f),,
       (PullbackPr1 P,,
        idpath (pr2 (P,, PullbackPr1 P · f))),,
       PullbackPr2 P,, PullbackSqrCommutes P) ⟧,
isaprop
  ((λ t : C / Z ⟦ Y,
          pr1
            ((P,, PullbackPr1 P · f),,
             (PullbackPr1 P,,
              idpath (pr2 (P,, PullbackPr1 P · f))),,
             PullbackPr2 P,, PullbackSqrCommutes P) ⟧,
    t
    · pr1
        (pr2
           ((P,, PullbackPr1 P · f),,
            (PullbackPr1 P,,
             idpath (pr2 (P,, PullbackPr1 P · f))),,
            PullbackPr2 P,, PullbackSqrCommutes P)) =
    j,, jeq
    × t
      · pr2
          (pr2
             ((P,, PullbackPr1 P · f),,
              (PullbackPr1 P,,
               idpath (pr2 (P,, PullbackPr1 P · f))),,
              PullbackPr2 P,, PullbackSqrCommutes P)) =
      k,, keq) y)
 abstract (intros h; apply isapropdirprod; apply has_homsets_slice_precat).
  
C: category
A, B, Z: C
f: C ⟦ A, Z ⟧
g: C ⟦ B, Z ⟧
P: Pullback f g
Y: C / Z
j: C ⟦ pr1 Y, pr1 (A,, f) ⟧

k: C ⟦ pr1 Y, pr1 (B,, g) ⟧

∏

      ((P,, PullbackPr1 P · f),,

        idpath (pr2 (P,, PullbackPr1 P · f))),,

(λ t : C / Z ⟦ Y,
       pr1

          PullbackPr2 P,, PullbackSqrCommutes P) ⟧,
 t
 · pr1
     (pr2
        ((P,, PullbackPr1 P · f),,
         (PullbackPr1 P,,
          idpath (pr2 (P,, PullbackPr1 P · f))),,
         PullbackPr2 P,, PullbackSqrCommutes P)) =
 j,, jeq
 × t
   · pr2
       (pr2
          ((P,, PullbackPr1 P · f),,
           (PullbackPr1 P,,
            idpath (pr2 (P,, PullbackPr1 P · f))),,
           PullbackPr2 P,, PullbackSqrCommutes P)) =
   k,, keq) y
→ y =
  PullbackArrow P (pr1 Y) j k
    (pullback_to_slice_binprod_subproof A B Z f g Y j
       jeq k keq),,
  pullback_to_slice_binprod_subproof0 A B Z f g P Y j
    jeq k keq
 abstract (intros h [H1 H2]; apply eq_mor_slicecat, PullbackArrowUnique;
             [ apply (maponpaths pr1 H1) | apply (maponpaths pr1 H2) ]).
Defined.

Definition BinProducts_slice_precat (PC : Pullbacks C) : ∏ x, BinProducts (C / x) :=
 λ x a b, pullback_to_slice_binprod (PC _ _ _ (pr2 a) (pr2 b)).

Definition Pullbacks_from_slice_BinProducts (BP : ∏ x, BinProducts (C / x)) : Pullbacks C :=
  λ x a b f g, slice_binprod_to_pullback (BP x (a ,, f) (b ,, g)).

End slicecat_binproducts.

        ⟦ BC (pr1 a) (pr1 b),,

            (pr2 a) (pr2 b), c ⟧,
(BinCoproductIn1 (BC (pr1 a) (pr1 b)),,
 BinCoproducts_slice_precat_subproof x a b) · fg = f
× (BinCoproductIn2 (BC (pr1 a) (pr1 b)),,
   BinCoproducts_slice_precat_subproof0 x a b) · fg =
  g

· pr2 c

    abstract (apply pathsinv0, BinCoproductArrowUnique;

      | rewrite assoc, (BinCoproductIn2Commutes C _ _ (BC (pr1 a) (pr1 b))), (pr2 g)]; apply idpath).

  BinCoproducts_slice_precat_subproof x a b) · t = f
 × (BinCoproductIn2 (BC (pr1 a) (pr1 b)),,
    BinCoproducts_slice_precat_subproof0 x a b) · t =
   g)

     (pr1 g),,

             [ apply BinCoproductIn1Commutes | apply BinCoproductIn2Commutes ]).

y : C / x
    ⟦ BC (pr1 a) (pr1 b),,
      BinCoproductArrow (BC (pr1 a) (pr1 b)) (pr2 a)

  ((λ t : C / x

     BinCoproducts_slice_precat_subproof x a b) · t =
    f

       BinCoproducts_slice_precat_subproof0 x a b) · t =

C: category
BC: BinCoproducts C
x: C
a, b, c: C / x

∏
y : C / x
    ⟦ BC (pr1 a) (pr1 b),,
      BinCoproductArrow (BC (pr1 a) (pr1 b)) (pr2 a)
        (pr2 b), c ⟧,
(λ t : C / x
       ⟦ BC (pr1 a) (pr1 b),,
         BinCoproductArrow (BC (pr1 a) (pr1 b))
           (pr2 a) (pr2 b), c ⟧,
 (BinCoproductIn1 (BC (pr1 a) (pr1 b)),,
  BinCoproducts_slice_precat_subproof x a b) · t = f
 × (BinCoproductIn2 (BC (pr1 a) (pr1 b)),,
    BinCoproducts_slice_precat_subproof0 x a b) · t =
   g) y
→ y =
  BinCoproductArrow (BC (pr1 a) (pr1 b)) (pr1 f)
    (pr1 g),,
  BinCoproducts_slice_precat_subproof1 x a b c f g
 abstract (intros y [<- <-]; apply eq_mor_slicecat, BinCoproductArrowUnique; apply idpath).
Defined.

End slicecat_bincoproducts.

Section slicecat_initial.

Local Notation "C / X" := (slice_cat C X).

x: C

x: C
C / x

x: C
C

IC: Initial C
x: C
(λ a : C, C ⟦ a, x ⟧) ?pr1

 apply (InitialObject IC).

(λ a : C, C ⟦ a, x ⟧) IC

IC: Initial C
x: C
y: C / x
C ⟦ IC, pr1 y ⟧
C: category
IC: Initial C
x: C
y: C / x
InitialArrow IC x = ?Goal · pr2 y

C: category

y: C / x

 apply InitialArrow.

C: category

→ y0 = InitialArrow IC (pr1 y)

 abstract (intros f ->; rewrite id_right; apply idpath).
Defined.

End slicecat_terminal.

(** Base change functor: https://ncatlab.org/nlab/show/base+change *)
Section base_change.

Context (C : category) (PC : Pullbacks C).

Local Notation "C / X" := (slice_cat C X).

 abstract (rewrite PullbackArrow_PullbackPr1; apply idpath).
Defined.

C: category
PC: Pullbacks C
c, c': C
g: C ⟦ c, c' ⟧
(λ _ : triangle_1_statement
         (slicecat_functor g,,
          base_change_functor g,, eta g,, eps g),
 triangle_2_statement
   (slicecat_functor g,,
    base_change_functor g,, eta g,, eps g))
  ((λ x : C / c,
    eq_mor_slicecat C c'
      (left_functor
         (slicecat_functor g,,
          base_change_functor g,, eta g,, eps g)
         (functor_identity (C / c) x))
      (functor_identity (C / c')
         (left_functor
            (slicecat_functor g,,
             base_change_functor g,, eta g,, eps g) x))
      (# (left_functor
            (slicecat_functor g,,
             base_change_functor g,, eta g,, eps g))
         (adjunit
            (slicecat_functor g,,
             base_change_functor g,, eta g,, eps g) x)
       · adjcounit
           (slicecat_functor g,,
            base_change_functor g,, eta g,, eps g)
           (left_functor
              (slicecat_functor g,,
               base_change_functor g,, eta g,, eps g)
              x))
      (identity
         (left_functor
            (slicecat_functor g,,
             base_change_functor g,, eta g,, eps g) x))
      (internal_paths_rew_r (C ⟦ pr1 x, pr1 x ⟧)
         (PullbackArrow
            (PC c' c (pr1 x) g (pr2 x · g)) (pr1 x)
            (pr2 x) (identity (pr1 x))
            (eta_data_subproof c c' g x)
          · PullbackPr2
              (PC c' c (pr1 x) g (pr2 x · g)))
         (identity (pr1 x))
         (λ p : C ⟦ pr1 x, pr1 x ⟧,
          p = identity (pr1 x))
         (idpath (identity (pr1 x)))
         (PullbackArrow_PullbackPr2
            (PC c' c (pr1 x) g (pr2 x · g)) (pr1 x)
            (pr2 x) (identity (pr1 x))
            (eta_data_subproof c c' g x))
       :
       pr1
         (# (left_functor
               (slicecat_functor g,,
                base_change_functor g,, eta g,, eps g))
            (adjunit
               (slicecat_functor g,,
                base_change_functor g,, eta g,, eps g)
               x)
          · adjcounit
              (slicecat_functor g,,
               base_change_functor g,, eta g,, eps g)
              (left_functor
                 (slicecat_functor g,,
                  base_change_functor g,,
                  eta g,, eps g) x)) =
       pr1
         (identity
            (left_functor
               (slicecat_functor g,,
                base_change_functor g,, eta g,, eps g)
               x))))
   :
   triangle_1_statement
     (slicecat_functor g,,
      base_change_functor g,, eta g,, eps g))

(** If the base change functor has a right adjoint, called dependent product, then C / c has
    exponentials. The formal proof is inspired by Proposition 2.1 from:
    https://ncatlab.org/nlab/show/locally+cartesian+closed+category#in_category_theory
*)
Section dependent_product.

Context (H : ∏ (c c' : C) (g : C⟦c,c'⟧), is_left_adjoint (base_change_functor g)).

Let dependent_product_functor {c c' : C} (g : C⟦c,c'⟧) :
  functor (C / c) (C / c') := right_adjoint (H c c' g).

Let BPC c : BinProducts (C / c) := @BinProducts_slice_precat C PC c.


C: category
PC: Pullbacks C
H: ∏ (c c' : C) (g : C ⟦ c, c' ⟧),
is_left_adjoint (base_change_functor g)
dependent_product_functor:= λ (c c' : C)
(g : C ⟦ c, c' ⟧),
right_adjoint (H c c' g): ∏ c c' : C,
C ⟦ c, c' ⟧
→ (C / c) ⟶ (C / c')
BPC:= λ c : C, BinProducts_slice_precat C PC c: ∏ c : C, BinProducts (C / c)
c: C
Af: C / c
constprod_functor1 (BPC c) Af =
base_change_functor (pr2 Af)
∙ slicecat_functor (pr2 Af)


C: category
PC: Pullbacks C
H: ∏ (c c' : C) (g : C ⟦ c, c' ⟧),
is_left_adjoint (base_change_functor g)
dependent_product_functor:= λ (c c' : C)
(g : C ⟦ c, c' ⟧),
right_adjoint (H c c' g): ∏ c c' : C,
C ⟦ c, c' ⟧
→ (C / c) ⟶ (C / c')
BPC:= λ c : C, BinProducts_slice_precat C PC c: ∏ c : C, BinProducts (C / c)
c: C
Af: C / c
constprod_functor1 (BPC c) Af =
base_change_functor (pr2 Af)
∙ slicecat_functor (pr2 Af)


C: category
PC: Pullbacks C

pr1
  (base_change_functor (pr2 Af)
   ∙ slicecat_functor (pr2 Af))

C: category
PC: Pullbacks C
H: ∏ (c c' : C) (g : C ⟦ c, c' ⟧),
is_left_adjoint (base_change_functor g)
dependent_product_functor:= λ (c c' : C)
(g : C ⟦ c, c' ⟧),

C ⟦ c, c' ⟧
→ (C / c) ⟶ (C / c')
BPC:= λ c : C, BinProducts_slice_precat C PC c: ∏ c : C, BinProducts (C / c)
c: C
Af: C / c
∏ (C1 C2 : C / c) (f : C / c ⟦ C1, C2 ⟧),
double_transport
  (((λ x : C / c,
     idpath
       (pr1
          (base_change_functor (pr2 Af)
           ∙ slicecat_functor (pr2 Af)) x))
    :
    pr1 (constprod_functor1 (BPC c) Af) ~
    pr1
      (base_change_functor (pr2 Af)
       ∙ slicecat_functor (pr2 Af))) C1)
  (((λ x : C / c,
     idpath
       (pr1
          (base_change_functor (pr2 Af)
           ∙ slicecat_functor (pr2 Af)) x))
    :
    pr1 (constprod_functor1 (BPC c) Af) ~
    pr1
      (base_change_functor (pr2 Af)
       ∙ slicecat_functor (pr2 Af))) C2)

pr2
  (pr1
     (base_change_functor (pr2 Af)
      ∙ slicecat_functor (pr2 Af))) C1 C2 f
 
C: category
PC: Pullbacks C
H: ∏ (c c' : C) (g : C ⟦ c, c' ⟧),
is_left_adjoint (base_change_functor g)
dependent_product_functor:= λ (c c' : C)
(g : C ⟦ c, c' ⟧),
right_adjoint (H c c' g): ∏ c c' : C,
C ⟦ c, c' ⟧
→ (C / c) ⟶ (C / c')
BPC:= λ c : C, BinProducts_slice_precat C PC c: ∏ c : C, BinProducts (C / c)
c: C
Af, x, y: C / c
f: C / c ⟦ x, y ⟧
PullbackArrow (PC c (pr1 Af) (pr1 y) (pr2 Af) (pr2 y))
  (PC c (pr1 Af) (pr1 x) (pr2 Af) (pr2 x))
  (PullbackPr1
     (PC c (pr1 Af) (pr1 x) (pr2 Af) (pr2 x))
   · identity (pr1 Af))
  (PullbackPr2
     (PC c (pr1 Af) (pr1 x) (pr2 Af) (pr2 x)) · pr1 f)
  (pullback_to_slice_binprod_subproof C (pr1 Af)
     (pr1 y) c (pr2 Af) (pr2 y) (BPC c Af x)
     (PullbackPr1
        (PC c (pr1 Af) (pr1 x) (pr2 Af) (pr2 x))
      · identity (pr1 Af))
     (comp_slice_precat_subproof C c
        (BinProductPr1 (C / c) (BPC c Af x))
        (identity Af))
     (PullbackPr2
        (PC c (pr1 Af) (pr1 x) (pr2 Af) (pr2 x))
      · pr1 f)
     (comp_slice_precat_subproof C c
        (BinProductPr2 (C / c) (BPC c Af x)) f)) =
PullbackArrow (PC c (pr1 Af) (pr1 y) (pr2 Af) (pr2 y))
  (PC c (pr1 Af) (pr1 x) (pr2 Af) (pr2 x))
  (PullbackPr1
     (PC c (pr1 Af) (pr1 x) (pr2 Af) (pr2 x)))
  (PullbackPr2
     (PC c (pr1 Af) (pr1 x) (pr2 Af) (pr2 x)) · pr1 f)
  (base_change_functor_data_subproof (pr1 Af) c
     (pr2 Af) x y f)

  
C: category
PC: Pullbacks C
H: ∏ (c c' : C) (g : C ⟦ c, c' ⟧),
is_left_adjoint (base_change_functor g)
dependent_product_functor:= λ (c c' : C)
(g : C ⟦ c, c' ⟧),
right_adjoint (H c c' g): ∏ c c' : C,
C ⟦ c, c' ⟧
→ (C / c) ⟶ (C / c')
BPC:= λ c : C, BinProducts_slice_precat C PC c: ∏ c : C, BinProducts (C / c)
c: C
Af, x, y: C / c
f: C / c ⟦ x, y ⟧
PullbackArrow (PC c (pr1 Af) (pr1 y) (pr2 Af) (pr2 y))
  (PC c (pr1 Af) (pr1 x) (pr2 Af) (pr2 x))
  (PullbackPr1
     (PC c (pr1 Af) (pr1 x) (pr2 Af) (pr2 x))
   · identity (pr1 Af))
  (PullbackPr2
     (PC c (pr1 Af) (pr1 x) (pr2 Af) (pr2 x)) · pr1 f)
  (pullback_to_slice_binprod_subproof C (pr1 Af)
     (pr1 y) c (pr2 Af) (pr2 y) (BPC c Af x)
     (PullbackPr1
        (PC c (pr1 Af) (pr1 x) (pr2 Af) (pr2 x))
      · identity (pr1 Af))
     (comp_slice_precat_subproof C c
        (BinProductPr1 (C / c) (BPC c Af x))
        (identity Af))
     (PullbackPr2
        (PC c (pr1 Af) (pr1 x) (pr2 Af) (pr2 x))
      · pr1 f)
     (comp_slice_precat_subproof C c
        (BinProductPr2 (C / c) (BPC c Af x)) f))
· PullbackPr1 (PC c (pr1 Af) (pr1 y) (pr2 Af) (pr2 y)) =
PullbackPr1 (PC c (pr1 Af) (pr1 x) (pr2 Af) (pr2 x))

   · identity (pr1 Af))
  (PullbackPr2
     (PC c (pr1 Af) (pr1 x) (pr2 Af) (pr2 x)) · 
   pr1 f)
  (pullback_to_slice_binprod_subproof C 
     (pr1 Af) (pr1 y) c 
     (pr2 Af) (pr2 y) 
     (BPC c Af x)
     (PullbackPr1
        (PC c (pr1 Af) (pr1 x) (pr2 Af) (pr2 x))

· pr1 f

 rewrite PullbackArrow_PullbackPr2; apply idpath.

(** ** Pullbacks *)

Section Pullbacks.
  Context {E : category} {I : ob E}.

  Local Notation "E / X" := (slice_cat E X).
  Local Notation "% A" := (slicecat_ob_object E I A) (at level 20).
  Local Notation "$ A" := (slicecat_ob_morphism E I A) (at level 20).
  Local Notation "$$ f" := (slicecat_mor_morphism E I f) (at level 21).

  (** A complex lemma statement for a simpler proof later *)
  
E: category
I: E
X: UU
P, Q, R: X → UU
xx: ∃! x : X, P x × Q x
(∏ x : X, isaprop (R x))
→ (∏ x : X, isaprop (P x))
  → (∏ x : X, isaprop (Q x))
    → R (pr1 (iscontrpr1 xx))
      → ∃! x : X, P x × Q x × R x

      → ∃! x : X, P x × Q x × R x

ispropQ: ∏ x : X, isaprop (Q x)
rxx: R (pr1 (iscontrpr1 xx))
∃! x : X, P x × Q x × R x

X: UU
P, Q, R: X → UU
xx: ∃! x : X, P x × Q x
ispropR: ∏ x : X, isaprop (R x)
ispropP: ∏ x : X, isaprop (P x)
ispropQ: ∏ x : X, isaprop (Q x)
rxx: R (pr1 (iscontrpr1 xx))
t: ∑ x : X, P x × Q x × R x
eq:= proofirrelevancecontr xx 
  (iscontrpr1 xx)
  (pr1 t,,
   make_dirprod (dirprod_pr1 (pr2 t))
     (dirprod_pr1 (dirprod_pr2 (pr2 t)))): iscontrpr1 xx =
pr1 t,,
make_dirprod (dirprod_pr1 (pr2 t))
  (dirprod_pr1 (dirprod_pr2 (pr2 t)))
pr1 t =
pr1
  (pr1 (iscontrpr1 xx),,
   dirprod_pr1 (pr2 (iscontrpr1 xx)),,
   dirprod_pr2 (pr2 (iscontrpr1 xx)),, rxx)

E: category
I: E
X: UU
P, Q, R: X → UU
xx: ∃! x : X, P x × Q x
ispropR: ∏ x : X, isaprop (R x)
ispropP: ∏ x : X, isaprop (P x)
ispropQ: ∏ x : X, isaprop (Q x)
rxx: R (pr1 (iscontrpr1 xx))
t: ∑ x : X, P x × Q x × R x
transportf (λ x : X, P x × Q x × R x)
  (let eq :=
     proofirrelevancecontr xx (iscontrpr1 xx)
       (pr1 t,,
        make_dirprod (dirprod_pr1 (pr2 t))
          (dirprod_pr1 (dirprod_pr2 (pr2 t)))) in
   ! (maponpaths pr1 eq @ idpath (pr1 t))) (pr2 t) =
pr2
  (pr1 (iscontrpr1 xx),,
   dirprod_pr1 (pr2 (iscontrpr1 xx)),,
   dirprod_pr2 (pr2 (iscontrpr1 xx)),, rxx)
 
E: category
I: E
X: UU
P, Q, R: X → UU
xx: ∃! x : X, P x × Q x
ispropR: ∏ x : X, isaprop (R x)
ispropP: ∏ x : X, isaprop (P x)
ispropQ: ∏ x : X, isaprop (Q x)
rxx: R (pr1 (iscontrpr1 xx))
t: ∑ x : X, P x × Q x × R x
isaprop
  (P
     (pr1
        (pr1 (iscontrpr1 xx),,
         dirprod_pr1 (pr2 (iscontrpr1 xx)),,
         dirprod_pr2 (pr2 (iscontrpr1 xx)),, rxx))
   × Q
       (pr1
          (pr1 (iscontrpr1 xx),,
           dirprod_pr1 (pr2 (iscontrpr1 xx)),,
           dirprod_pr2 (pr2 (iscontrpr1 xx)),, rxx))
     × R
         (pr1
            (pr1 (iscontrpr1 xx),,
             dirprod_pr1 (pr2 (iscontrpr1 xx)),,
             dirprod_pr2 (pr2 (iscontrpr1 xx)),, rxx)))

        do 2 (apply isapropdirprod; auto).
  Qed.

      (** In two steps, we reduce the problem of a pullback in [E/I] to that of
          a pullback in [E] (which we already have).

          1. Simplify the equalities involved in the sigma-type.
          2. Note that what is required is simply a pullback in [E] with
             an extra commutation condition.
       *)
      
E: category
I: E
A, B, C: E / I
k: E / I ⟦ A, C ⟧
l: E / I ⟦ B, C ⟧
PB: Pullback ($$ k) ($$ l)
eq: PullbackPr1 PB · $ A = PullbackPr2 PB · $ B
PBtoI:= PullbackPr1 PB · $ A: E ⟦ PB, I ⟧
PB': E / I
prA': E / I ⟦ PB', A ⟧
prB': E / I ⟦ PB', B ⟧
commSq': prA' · k = prB' · l
(∑ hk : E / I ⟦ PB', PB,, PBtoI ⟧,
 hk
 · (PullbackPr1 PB,, idpath (PullbackPr1 PB · pr2 A)) =
 prA' × hk · (PullbackPr2 PB,, eq) = prB')
≃ (∑ kk : E ⟦ % PB', PB ⟧,
   kk · PullbackPr1 PB = $$ prA'
   × kk · PullbackPr2 PB = $$ prB'
     × $ PB' = kk · PBtoI)

I: E
A, B, C: E / I
k: E / I ⟦ A, C ⟧
l: E / I ⟦ B, C ⟧
PB: Pullback ($$ k) ($$ l)
eq: PullbackPr1 PB · $ A = PullbackPr2 PB · $ B
PBtoI:= PullbackPr1 PB · $ A: E ⟦ PB, I ⟧
PB': E / I
prA': E / I ⟦ PB', A ⟧
prB': E / I ⟦ PB', B ⟧
commSq': prA' · k = prB' · l
∃! kk : E ⟦ % PB', PB ⟧,
kk · PullbackPr1 PB = $$ prA'
× kk · PullbackPr2 PB = $$ prB' × $ PB' = kk · PBtoI

      
E: category
I: E
A, B, C: E / I
k: E / I ⟦ A, C ⟧
l: E / I ⟦ B, C ⟧
PB: Pullback ($$ k) ($$ l)
eq: PullbackPr1 PB · $ A = PullbackPr2 PB · $ B
PBtoI:= PullbackPr1 PB · $ A: E ⟦ PB, I ⟧
PB': E / I
prA': E / I ⟦ PB', A ⟧
prB': E / I ⟦ PB', B ⟧
commSq': prA' · k = prB' · l
UU
 exact (∑ kk : PB' --> (PullbackObject PB,, PBtoI),
                ($$ kk) · PullbackPr1 PB = ($$ prA') ×
                ($$ kk) · PullbackPr2 PB = ($$ prB')).
      
E: category
I: E
A, B, C: E / I
k: E / I ⟦ A, C ⟧
l: E / I ⟦ B, C ⟧
PB: Pullback ($$ k) ($$ l)
eq: PullbackPr1 PB · $ A = PullbackPr2 PB · $ B
PBtoI:= PullbackPr1 PB · $ A: E ⟦ PB, I ⟧
PB': E / I
prA': E / I ⟦ PB', A ⟧
prB': E / I ⟦ PB', B ⟧
commSq': prA' · k = prB' · l
(∑ hk : E / I ⟦ PB', PB,, PBtoI ⟧,
 hk
 · (PullbackPr1 PB,, idpath (PullbackPr1 PB · pr2 A)) =
 prA' × hk · (PullbackPr2 PB,, eq) = prB')
≃ (∑ kk : E / I ⟦ PB', PB,, PBtoI ⟧,
   $$ kk · PullbackPr1 PB = $$ prA'
   × $$ kk · PullbackPr2 PB = $$ prB')

prB': E / I ⟦ PB', B ⟧
commSq': prA' · k = prB' · l
x: E / I ⟦ PB', PB,, PBtoI ⟧

prA' × x · (PullbackPr2 PB,, eq) = prB'
≃ $$ x · PullbackPr1 PB = $$ prA'
  × $$ x · PullbackPr2 PB = $$ prB'

E: category
I: E
A, B, C: E / I
k: E / I ⟦ A, C ⟧
l: E / I ⟦ B, C ⟧
PB: Pullback ($$ k) ($$ l)
eq: PullbackPr1 PB · $ A = PullbackPr2 PB · $ B
PBtoI:= PullbackPr1 PB · $ A: E ⟦ PB, I ⟧
PB': E / I
prA': E / I ⟦ PB', A ⟧
prB': E / I ⟦ PB', B ⟧
commSq': prA' · k = prB' · l
(∑ kk : E / I ⟦ PB', PB,, PBtoI ⟧,
 $$ kk · PullbackPr1 PB = $$ prA'
 × $$ kk · PullbackPr2 PB = $$ prB')
≃ (∑ kk : E ⟦ % PB', PB ⟧,
   kk · PullbackPr1 PB = $$ prA'
   × kk · PullbackPr2 PB = $$ prB'
     × $ PB' = kk · PBtoI)

E: category
I: E
A, B, C: E / I
k: E / I ⟦ A, C ⟧
l: E / I ⟦ B, C ⟧
PB: Pullback ($$ k) ($$ l)
eq: PullbackPr1 PB · $ A = PullbackPr2 PB · $ B
PBtoI:= PullbackPr1 PB · $ A: E ⟦ PB, I ⟧
PB': E / I
prA': E / I ⟦ PB', A ⟧
prB': E / I ⟦ PB', B ⟧
commSq': prA' · k = prB' · l
(∑ (x : E ⟦ % PB', PB ⟧) (p : $ PB' = x · PBtoI),
 (λ kk : slicecat_mor E I PB' (PB,, PBtoI),
  $$ kk · PullbackPr1 PB = $$ prA'
  × $$ kk · PullbackPr2 PB = $$ prB') (x,, p))
≃ (∑ kk : E ⟦ % PB', PB ⟧,
   kk · PullbackPr1 PB = $$ prA'
   × kk · PullbackPr2 PB = $$ prB'
     × $ PB' = kk · PBtoI)

eq: PullbackPr1 PB · $ A = PullbackPr2 PB · $ B
PBtoI:= PullbackPr1 PB · $ A: E ⟦ PB, I ⟧
PB': E / I
prA': E / I ⟦ PB', A ⟧
prB': E / I ⟦ PB', B ⟧
commSq': prA' · k = prB' · l
$ PB' = pr1 prA' · $ A

          apply slicecat_mor_comm.
  Defined.
